Shen Bao Radio Weekly

Skip Distance in Shortwave Communication 247

— Chongling

Shortwave radio communication, with its ability to achieve long-distance communication with low power, has been valued by the radio community. Moreover, because it has many advantages over longwave, shortwave communication today has a tendency to replace longwave. How can we ignore this rapidly developing shortwave communication?

The characteristics of shortwave propagation are very interesting. The most obvious phenomenon that shortwave communication cannot ignore is the so-called "skip distance." The propagation of shortwave depends on its high frequency. The radio waves propagating along the ground are absorbed by the ground, and the power attenuates very quickly. After only a short distance of thirty or fifty miles, it is too weak to be distinguished. Therefore, shortwave is not as good as longwave. The part that travels along the ground is not applicable except for extremely short-distance communication. Shortwave relies entirely on the part that is emitted into the sky. This part of the radio wave directly hits the Heaviside layer in the sky. Because the Heaviside layer has reflection ability, it can be reflected from the Heaviside layer to the ground. The distance reached by this reflected radio wave is quite far, so it is used for shortwave communication. However, there is a distance between the reach of the direct wave and the reach of the reflected wave from the Heaviside layer. Within this distance, the radio wave propagating along the ground has long disappeared, and the reflected radio wave has passed over it. Therefore, there is no sound. This distance is named skip distance. Therefore, if a receiver is installed within the skip distance, it will not be able to receive audio, which is a major shortcoming of shortwave communication.

Skip distance is deeply related to wavelength, elevation angle of radio waves, and the height and electron density of the Heaviside layer. There is a reason for the change in skip distance with wavelength, day and night, time, and season. According to the results of theory and experimentation, the following relationships have been obtained:

(1) Wavelength: Under the same height of the Heaviside layer, the skip distance increases as the wavelength decreases, as shown in Figure 1. According to experiments, the Heaviside layer at a height of 100 miles is expected to have no skip distance with a wavelength of 80 meters; with a wavelength of 40 meters, the skip distance is about 100 miles; with a wavelength of 20 meters, the skip distance is about 500 miles; with a wavelength of 10 meters, the skip distance increases to 1,000 to 2,000 miles. For a Heaviside layer of 225 miles high, there still seems to be no skip distance with a wavelength of 80 meters; if the wavelength is reduced to 40 meters, the skip distance is about 200 miles; 20 meters is 1,000 miles; and at a wavelength of 10 meters, the transmitted radio wave penetrates deep into the Heaviside layer and can never return to the ground. The reason why ultra-short waves cannot be used for long-distance communication is because of this. The skip distance has such a relationship with the wavelength. Therefore, there is a reason why audio of 40 meters can be received in a certain place, but audio of 36 meters wavelength emitted from the same place cannot be received. (To be continued)

Simple Method to Increase Variable Capacitor Capacitance 248

— Yongyan

There are many ways to increase the capacity of a variable capacitor, but the method described here is relatively the simplest and most economical. Because we know that two sets of metal plates separated by an insulator become a capacitor; the capacity of this capacitor is directly proportional to the dielectric constant of the insulator. Therefore, we can increase the capacity simply by replacing it with another insulator with a higher dielectric constant.

The dielectric constant of air is 1, mica is 4 to 8, wax is 2 to 2.5, porcelain is 4.4, quartz is 4.5, rosin is 2.5, shellac is 3.1, ordinary glass is 3.1 to 4, and bakelite is 5 to 6.

For example, if we want to increase the capacity of a 0.0001 air-insulated variable capacitor to 0.00025 Farads, then we only need to fill all the gaps between the metal plates of the capacitor with wax. If the increase is less than 0.00025, then less wax should be poured in.

In short, to increase the capacity a lot, use an insulator with a larger dielectric constant and fill all the gaps between the metal plates; otherwise, use an insulator with a smaller constant and only fill part of the gaps. The exact number is best determined by experimentation.

Satisfactory Single-Tube Amplifier Speaker Circuit 249

— Cao Runsheng

Recently, a friend asked me to install an AC amplifier speaker radio for him. I thought this was another opportunity for experimentation, so I readily agreed. Because I had heard friends say that the Megadyne circuit is very reliable, I chose the following circuit. It took a full half day to install it. I plugged in the power supply and turned it on, feeling doubtful. It really made me jump with joy. It was able to play all the large and small local radio stations in the speaker. The volume is comparable to that of an ordinary three-tube radio. As for selectivity, it is also considerable because a filter was added. I think this circuit must also be very much needed by amateur comrades, so I specially introduce it. I hope that amateur comrades will announce the results after the experiment, which would be very fortunate.

Simple Method for Matching the Impedance of the Speaker Field Coil 250

— Pao

The field coil of the speaker in commercial radios also serves as a filtering choke coil in the substituting B power supply. Therefore, it has a certain impedance value and cannot be changed casually, otherwise the output substituting B voltage will change and affect the operation of the radio. For this reason, sometimes the field coil is damaged, and a speaker with the same impedance cannot be found for a while, then the entire radio will have to be put aside.

When encountering this difficulty, the following method can be used to solve it. Just remove the original speaker and replace it with the two items shown in the attached figure. In the figure, L is a newly replaced power speaker field coil, its impedance is smaller than that of this machine; R is a 10-watt wire-wound resistor, its impedance value plus L should be equal to the impedance of the original speaker's field coil. If hum occurs after this modification, then the dotted line part in the figure should be added. C is a paper fixed capacitor with a capacity of 2 MFD, and the withstand voltage is the same as the filtering capacitor in the substitute B power supply part of this radio.

Knowledge that Beginners Should Have (1) (Continued) 251

— Yang Xuelun

(3) Capacitors: Variable capacitors are often used in radios to adjust the frequency. These capacitors should be air-insulated and have a straight-line frequency. When assembling a single-tube radio, although only one variable capacitor is needed, a dual-gang or triple-gang capacitor can be purchased in advance for future expansion needs, and matched with a suitable slow-rotation dial. Do not buy inferior products for this type of capacitor, because they are easily damaged and the capacitance of the two capacitors cannot be synchronized. Although there is a compensator, it will eventually lead to problems after assembly. There is no way to remedy it except to discard and repurchase it. Therefore, be careful when purchasing. The capacity of variable capacitors is usually 0.00035 and 0.0005 MFD. The former requires a higher ratio of primary to secondary coils, so the efficiency is also higher. Fixed capacitors, except those used for filtering, should be mica-insulated to avoid losses.

(4) Coils: The coils mentioned in this article include high and low frequency transformers, detector coils, and high and low frequency chokes. Assuming that the radio we hope to build has one stage of high-frequency amplification, one stage of detection, and one stage of low-frequency amplification, then the high-frequency amplification and detection coils can be wound on spiderweb boards, because their efficiency is indeed higher than that of cylindrical coils. If high-frequency amplification needs to be used for two or more stages, then cylindrical coils must be used due to spatial constraints. Moreover, if the number of high-frequency amplification stages is increased, even if there is a slight loss, it will not be noticed. It is best to use silk-covered wire for self-made coils. Enameled wire can also be used, but it cannot be disassembled and modified, because once it is disassembled and modified, the insulating paint will fall off in some places, so it cannot be used. When winding coils, it is better to wind a few more turns first, and remove the excess. Otherwise, adding windings during wiring will not only damage the appearance, but also reduce efficiency. Low-frequency transformers are very important to sound quality and volume, and must be high-quality products. A ratio of 3.5:1 is the most suitable. High-frequency chokes should be purchased with segmented winding methods, such as those produced by America's Zhongyong, otherwise it is better not to use them. Low-frequency chokes must pay attention to their inductance and the current value that can pass through them, depending on their use.

(5) Resistors: Resistors are divided into two types: variable and fixed. In terms of materials, there are also carbon and wire-wound types. Generally, carbon is used for high resistance values, and wire-wound is used for low resistance values. Variable resistors with high resistance values are also called potentiometers, and are often used to adjust volume or control voltage. This device should also be high-quality. The fixed resistors with high resistance values are grid leaks. Their values should not be strictly adhered to the values ​​stated on the circuit diagram. Replacing and testing with 1 to 4 megohms can often yield better results. Carbon resistors with less than one megohm are mostly used for voltage reduction. Manufacturers often paint various colors on the outside to indicate their numerical values. When purchasing, pay attention to the ohm and watt values. Wire-wound variable resistors are mostly used to control filament current, and fixed ones are used for both C resistors and voltage dividers. (To be continued)

The elderly are neighbors with the spittoon, young men are close to women, and young children are fond of leather toys. Because the objects they are fond of are different, their tastes of joy and sorrow are separated into a path of heaven and earth.

A person who can kill is not necessarily a bandit. Bandits killing people is very obvious. In society, there is a kind of people with human faces and animal hearts. A Journey to Nantianshan 253

— Liu Li

Nantianshan is located 120 li south of Qingtian County. Taoist books call it the Fourth Blessed Land, covering an area of more than 200 li. There are many plains in the middle. The mountains are steep and the water flows from flying springs. The water of the whole mountain converges from hundreds of streams and flows out from five mouths. (There is also a northeast mouth outside the east, west, south, and north mouths.) The mouths are all towering peaks, exceptionally majestic and beautiful. The waterfalls are especially spectacular, with three places over 1,000 feet high and many places over 100 feet high. Nantianxiang is located in the center of it all. Tourists can view the scenery in Nantianxiang for several days and the food and lodging are relatively comfortable. There are four ways to enter the mountain: (1) Take a boat from Qingtian City to Baiyan, which is 80 li and can be reached in one day. Hire a sedan to enter the mountain and climb the Stone Ladder Ridge from the Wanfu Mouth on the east side. It takes half a day to reach Nantianxiang, which is 50 li. (2) Hire a boat from Qingtian City to go up the Xiaoxi River to the foot of the mountain, which is 110 li. Stay overnight in the boat and cross the He Kou Ridge (one of the Nine Ridges) the next day to Wuyang Village, the hometown of Liu Wencheng, which is 20 li. It is another 10 li to Nantianxiang. Although the journey is longer, the scenery is the best. (3) Take a sedan from Qingtian City to Nantianxiang via Dalingfu, which is 120 li and can be reached in one and a half days. The journey is the shortest, but there is not much scenery along the way. (4) Take an early bus from Ruian City to Pingyangkeng, which takes 3 hours and is 70 li. Hire a sedan to go through the port to Dayu, which takes a full day and is 140 li. Then take a sedan up Dahui Ridge, which takes 3 hours. The most famous Baizhang Waterfall in Xinting Mountain is nearby. It is another 30 li to Nantianxiang. In total, there are 32 peaks in the whole mountain, with Wanren, Shipu, Kangwu, and Wuyang being the best. The most magnificent waterfall is Baizhangji, and the most ingenious is Chuanliang Waterfall. The best cave is the Water Curtain at the North Mouth. Du Mu Taihe's poem about traveling to Nantian, "Deep in the mountains in May, there are sheepskins," shows that the mountain is high and airy, making it a famous summer resort. The best time to travel to the mountain is in summer.

Wife's Comfort 254

— Chen Liang

Returning home from outside, putting down my lecture folder, a slender, ink-black shadow follows me, carrying a faint fragrance of Cymbidium orchids. A bit of irritability evaporated by liver qi naturally subsides. At home, my wife always loves to wear a long black silk dress, black stockings, and black leather shoes. A pair of black earrings peek out from under her feet, clinging to her white cheeks. That clear facial contour and graceful demeanor rejuvenate a body exhausted from work. However, the comfort my wife gives me is more than just these.

Friends say I am happy—a happily married husband. I, too, admit this. I don't have to take off my coat myself. When I sit down, a cup of tea, neither too strong nor too weak, made with pre-Qingming tea leaves, and a cigarette that I love to smoke, are personally handed to me by her. When eating, there is a plate of fried eggs and a bowl of pure vegetable soup she personally prepares. She seems to be the worm in my stomach, having the same tongue and the same mood as me. However, she is much more patient than I am. When I am angry, she sits to the side and smiles faintly.

"If you continue to be so docile, you'll become your husband's slave!" Someone said to her, trying to provoke her. However, she is unmoved. She remains docile in my presence. In the evening, I never see my wife go to bed and sleep before I do. Sometimes when I come home late, she'll be dozing off at my desk. I feel both ashamed and remorseful. Therefore, I often force myself to go home earlier. Isn't it true that my wife is preparing many comforting actions and words, waiting for me to accept them?

"I would rather be docile to a faithful husband until death," my wife once said.

Mr. Broad's Daydream 255

— Jiang Mi

Records of Lingering Fragrance 256

— Original by Princess Der Ling of Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

When the colors were dyed and the silk was dried, the results reached a very satisfactory level. Thus, these silks were taken down one by one from the frames and wound onto wooden bobbins, usually one bobbin for each color. After winding, since they were not used for weaving silk, they could only be kept as materials for embroidery or sewing. However, so much was not needed at once, so they were stored first, to be selected and used according to the colors specified when the seamstresses needed them.

The description of the silk-making process can be said to be complete up to this point. Next, we will talk about the shoe-making industry in the palace. Although the shoes worn daily by women of some status in the palace were made by dedicated shoe-making artisans, the main purpose of supporting these artisans in the palace was really for the Empress Dowager alone. Therefore, the narrative here focuses on the phoenix shoes worn by the Empress Dowager.

Speaking of the Empress Dowager's phoenix shoes, readers should not think it is a small topic. If we were to explain it in detail from beginning to end, there would be a lot to write about! First, let's talk about the management aspect: there were two eunuchs who were specially assigned to manage the Empress Dowager's phoenix shoes all year round without doing anything else. They did not feel that this task was easy; they felt it was very important. They dared not slack off at all, and they always carefully guarded these phoenix shoes, as if they were guarding a treasure house. According to the facts, the Empress Dowager's phoenix shoes could indeed be considered a valuable treasure, because most of the phoenix shoes had extremely valuable jewels, jade, or emeralds inlaid on them, and they were by no means ordinary things. (286)

Critique 257

— Hu Ping

Unable to afford books, I can only go to the library. The library is a soup kitchen for poor boys (of course, the rich can go too). It is truly great compassion and boundless merit. Unexpectedly, many talented people who read books (perhaps beauties do not) especially like to write a few lines of criticism in the books. They treat the books in the library as the walls of a public toilet, commenting at will. It can be said that every sentence is wonderful and every word is clever. Here are a few excerpts for everyone to enjoy together.

One day, I found a book by Dewey called "The School of Tomorrow" with three lines written in fountain pen:

"Tomorrow: Students sit on a large platform to listen to lectures, and the teacher teaches on a small stool. The day after tomorrow: Students give the questions, and the teacher takes the test. The day after that: There are no teachers in the school."

I was praising, "Excellent, excellent!" Unexpectedly, there was also something written on the blank space on the side of another page:

"Tomorrow, all universities, middle schools, and elementary schools will be co-educational. The day after tomorrow, men and women will take classes shirtless. The day after that: Men and women will take classes naked."

These two people each have their own merits. Also, in Kilpatrick's "Philosophy of Education," I saw: "The method of the school is nothing more than inviting celebrities to be school directors, building foreign-style school buildings, and often performing or dancing, or participating in propaganda and shouting slogans."

These are all facts, but I think this gentleman is wasting ink. In the Complete Works of Ryunosuke Akutagawa, someone wrote a poem: "Kikuchi's fame is passed down after death, Natsume cherished his talent in those years. Since Kappa became a final echo, the daughters of Tokyo have lingering grief." And on a volume of "Sha Ran" someone wrote: "I can write human joys and sorrows, but I am ashamed that my talent is not as unrestrained. Hearing the roar of the snow mountain lion, I read strange books with blood on my skull." Both poems are excellent and written in the same handwriting; the writing is also very charming.

In Andreev's "The Seven Who Were Hanged," there are also two very funny sentences. One line is: "Pitiful. Even my sister-in-law became eight!" Another line notes: "My sister-in-law has big eyes and a thin neck, just like a hanged ghost."

The strangest thing is that in "Abelard and Heloise's Letters," someone wrote: "What's so strange about monks and nuns getting along? We in China have had it for a long time!" Reading it, one can't help but laugh.

Little Knowledge

Small Commandments for Eating Western Food 258

— Zhang Feng

Eating Western food (the common name for Western cuisine) is like tasting exotic flavors, and is often equated with riding in cars and living in foreign houses. Living a Europeanized life, isn't it enjoyable! However, there are those who are not familiar with its customs, and often cause ridicule among the elegant (also written as "爷," similar in meaning to "freehand style"). Although this is a trivial matter, there are some points that should be warned. Those who are familiar with it and do not lose their etiquette are the so-called gentlemen. Otherwise, if you eat Western food with the intention of having fun, and make a joke with nowhere to seek justice, is it worth it? I still remember when I was a child, I received instructions from Ms. Highland of the United States, and recorded the following points based on the common mistakes, and added my own opinions:—

Do not talk much when eating. — This is the same meaning as Confucius's legacy "Don't speak when eating" in our country, which shows that many things in China and foreign countries, ancient and modern, have similarities. The intention is probably: If you talk during a meal, you will force the people at the same table to listen and respond perfunctorily, which will interfere with eating — this is a kind of tyranny! Also, talking during a meal inevitably changes the normal state of eating, such as neglecting chewing, speeding up swallowing, reducing the amount of food, etc., which ultimately affects human health. However, there are often impromptu speeches at large banquets now, which can often give the audience at the same table more than they lose, so let's discuss it separately.

Do not bend your neck to eat from the plate. — Only beasts eat by bringing their mouths to the food. The reason why there are stiff collars in the clothes of the two people is probably to maintain the posture of keeping the neck straight.

Do not put the tip of the knife into your mouth. — The comedy of a country bumpkin cutting his tongue while eating Western food is because the barbarian did not pay attention to this commandment.

It is forbidden to strike the knife and fork against each other, or to make a sound by striking the utensils. — Although this sound has the beauty of music, it is not needed at the dining table. After Liu Bang of the Han Dynasty gained the world, he only granted his nephew the title of Marquis of Jie Geng after repeated requests from his subordinates, just so as not to forget the old evil of his sister-in-law banging the spoon on the side of the pot to indicate that there was nothing left, and Feng Huan sang and sighed "No fish in one meal"; therefore, although the sound of these eating utensils may not all be to express injustice, they are often enough to cause unnecessary misunderstandings, so it is better to be quiet.

The sound of a knife and fork touching the bottom of the bowl, making a sound like filing copper, makes people's teeth sour and their skin crawl, and is most likely to cause disgust — this kind of tooth-grinding sound is probably unbearable for any nation, and is very annoying!

Do not make sounds of chewing lips or sucking tongue. — This is the ugly state of gluttony, excessively revealing his ability to ravage food, and taking pleasure in himself. There are also those who chew wantonly when eating, unconsciously making this kind of sound between his mouth and tongue, as if it is the rhythm of a proud eye sound, which makes people speculate that he cannot often get a rich meal, bringing this kind of poor appearance. This kind of eating appearance is also not allowed in China.

Do not make a sucking sound when eating soup — Even swarms of mosquitoes can form thunder. If everyone at the meal makes a loud sound of sucking soup, don't make people suspect that it is the sound of a surging tide?

Little Western Paradise 259

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Eleven: Night Talk of a Sad Life, Originally a Dream / Footprints Scattered, Wind and Rain Too Oppressive

Huanhua said, "Alas! Mr. Li, you are a well-fed person who doesn't know the hunger of the hungry. For people like us, it's already amazing if someone looks at us twice, so how dare we talk about any conditions with others? I'm just begging Mr. Jia to do a good deed and take me back to Jiangnan by the way. I have nothing to repay him with, so I'm going to be a matchmaker for him now. I think that Miss Zhu's family must have some grievances that are inconvenient to tell men. If I go and talk to her carefully and get her thoughts out, then I can know what it would take for her to be satisfied. If we can do it, we'll persuade Mr. Jia to do it. If we can't do it, we'll persuade Miss Zhu's family to let go, and wouldn't this matter be successful?" Li Shilian said, "What you said is not bad. We also thought of some things, but it's not convenient to say them to the girl. Her mother is not worth mentioning, she doesn't know anything at all. As for that Sister-in-law Hu, she wants to make a fortune from it, and she wants to talk about her price before she drops other people's affairs. It's better not to talk about this matter, the more you talk about it, the more trouble it will be. You have a way with words, I think, if you are willing to come forward, this matter will definitely be successful." Huanhua smiled and said, "How do you know that I have a way with words?" Li Shilian didn't say anything, first he nodded towards the room next door, and then he whispered, "This gentleman is extremely shrewd, ordinary people are not easy to move. But..." Huanhua waved her hands at him repeatedly, and smiled with a pursed mouth. At this time, there was already a sound from the room next door, presumably Jia Duocai had already gotten up. Li Shilian had many things to ask of Jia Duocai, so it was not convenient for him to talk here for too long, lest he offend someone, so he immediately walked out of the room lightly, and then walked towards Jia Duocai's room with a heavy pace. Afterwards, Yang Huanhua reapplied her makeup and also walked towards this side. (175)

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Small Sensations of Qingming 260

— Li Min

The spring is bright, and the Qingming Festival is coming soon. This is the best season of the year. Schools are on vacation, and the mountains and fields are dotted with people enjoying the spring. Parks are also crowded with people, and everyone has a happy energy on their faces. Spring is truly a happy season.

The most interesting thing is sweeping tombs during Qingming. In the countryside, the fields are full of flying paper ashes. Although the people who sweep tombs are all mourning the dead, they all have a bit of joyful spring feeling on their faces. It is actually a kind of pastime used to enjoy the spring. It is not impossible to say that.

Speaking of sweeping tombs, I remembered the National Tomb Sweeping Day decided by the Central Government that I saw in the newspaper a few days ago. The so-called National Tomb Sweeping Day is when the Central Government sends personnel to the northwest to sweep and worship the tombs of the ancient Yellow Emperor and others, as a kind of commemoration of our forgetting the ancestors of the nation, hence the name National Tomb Sweeping Day. This is very interesting. Our national spirit has indeed declined and is on the verge of exhaustion. The country is full of foreign iron hooves and bloodstains. If we don't commemorate our national ancestors, this nation will not be far from destruction.

However, restoring the national spirit and national power seems to be not enough to rely solely on some spiritual commemorations and memories. It is best to take out our strength and wash away the bloodstains and wounds all over this nation, then there may be hope. In addition to the Central Government's decision to have a National Tomb Sweeping Day this time, we hope that there will be a more meaningful move for the people to strive for.

Small Scenes of Hanshi 261

— Xu Xizhen

Around noon, the bell of a distant temple rang out "Dang——". The faint sound drifted across the fields, over the eaves of farmhouses, and over the cemetery with scattered weeds.

In the cemetery, some ashes of paper money, along with the swaying of willow branches, and the ripples of the stream, flew up rhythmically, scattering the remaining fragments on some ownerless desolate tombs. The fields were silent, and one could hear the beat of one's heart, and three or two faint whispers of unknown birds in the distance.

As the wind passed, it brought one or two faint, lingering cries—a remembrance and recollection of the dear departed soul. From this, I seemed to hear some notes of friendship and memory between people; perhaps it was a young widow remaining in the world, remembering the dreamlike past love, and now, she could only fall in a pile of grass in front of the tomb, searching for the cherry-colored smile of that year in sobbing tears? Perhaps it was; the younger generation, at the moment of losing the courage and meaning of survival, walked in front of the deceased elders to remember the appearance and feelings of this dead generation, and in the tears of an orphan that no one can accept, to recall the peaceful medieval mood? Or perhaps it was some people with greater, more meaningful ideals, who, in the advancing spring, chose this day more suitable for remembrance, bringing blood-colored flowers to dedicate to this friend who threw himself into the light, but was finally eroded by boundless darkness, while at the same time, in tears, reckoning some great, terrible past sufferings that are not suitable for people to know, and predicting those future, unimaginable storms? But, who knows? The relationship between people is mysterious, infinite, and far-reaching beyond measure! When people are alive, they play all kinds of postures of life as much as possible according to their own ways, and when one day they complete the task of the drama of life, and suddenly drill into the cemetery that serves as the backstage of the natural world, all actions have formed one ten-thousandth of history, and all friendships? They can only be found in the low and distant crying in the silent cemetery in a dark spring day.

Could it be said that: is this thousands of sobs that floats in the cemetery during the Cold Food Festival also a kind of glory in the world?

(From some unknown place, a cuckoo cried out once or twice, and a drizzle was falling in the fields.

I really want to ask: where is there a wine shop with an apricot-yellow flag, using the true laughter of the human world to treat people?)

The mud road gradually became wet, and people felt an unpleasant feeling of mud when they stepped on it. By the stream, the willow branches silently brushed the water surface, and peach blossoms also jumped into the water like stars. People on their way, with an anxious and hurried heart, hurried across the sticky dirt road, looking at the sky. Grey, low-hanging, dull and suffocating! So he reached out to brush off the rain falling on his body, and grumbled unhappily to himself: "Damn, I didn't bring an umbrella, I didn't bring rain shoes or oilskin, such a good day, it rained for no reason, who would have thought of it! Who would have thought of it? Strange!

On the dirt road, wheelbarrows were walking sparsely, the wheels intermittently making a scattered, unpleasant, ear-piercing sound. People who swept tombs returned with a desolate mood, and middle-aged servants carried the leftover food and sacrificial utensils, following silently. It was already the time when the sun was resting on the west mountain, and dusk gradually rose, covering the entire drizzling field. Somewhere, crows were cawing in the evening.

Another windy and rainy Cold Food Festival sank into the setting sun.

Streamlined Life 262

— Cheng Quan

People living in this brand new and rotten 1935, even their lifestyles have been changed to streamlined——isn't that right? These days, everyone is like that: living today without knowing tomorrow——maybe today they are still walking on a very flat road, and tomorrow they will be thrown into the deep valley of life; but, who dares to think about the perspective of "tomorrow's" life anymore——that's stupid. Because, maybe tomorrow is already...?

(The streets of the big metropolis in the morning have a crowded "Rush bour" to the office. Cars and people, like the early tide of the Yellow Sea, flow in the same direction. People's minds are filled with: the news headlines on the morning newspaper, the real faces of the foreign managers in the foreign firm, the numbers in the ledger, the "number" for salary, the calculation of the months of arrears: January, February...

The tram rings its bell constantly like a death knell, crawling slowly like a snake. The carriages are crowded, and people are packed into boxes like sardines. It's hot, and full of uncomfortable human atmosphere, suffocating and dizzying.

Page 20

When the car stopped for the Xth time in front of the red light of the traffic light, you could hear the voice of or someone talking in the third-class carriage:

——In short, I say, things are not good this year; living this year is like fighting guerrillas, called: living one day is one day; otherwise, who can calculate the fate of tomorrow? ——Silenced, an uncomfortable feeling stirred in my heart: At this time yesterday, I was still sitting in the car going to the foreign firm to sign in, and who would have thought that by noon, the four words "cost savings" would break my rice bowl under the qualification of twelve years——this is simply a dream, a dream! A dream that no one would believe! But the fact is unmistakable——wasn't I no longer taking the car to the office today, but instead going to find someone to "help"?

——This nightmare-like, streamlined life ah)

Many people, countless people, put on 1935-style coats, hurrying, running, and carefully running on the tight string of this streamlined era: in between, there is the wolf-like ambition and the rabbit's cunning of the enterprise, and the result is sinking into the sorrow of decline. The small clerks are running desperately on the track of life with a wet heart, selling their labor day by day and filling their stomachs half full under the pickaxe. The clerks are dizzy by the keyboard of the typewriter, and the politicians train the patients to be as beautiful and fluent as Kroemi's furniture. So: the streamlined beauty of 1935 appears in people's cries, people's laughter, and people's planning. The new era is streamlined, people live in the middle, people are happy, people are sad, people are drunk in the dimples of sleeping pills.

(Reflecting, the bankrupt department store owner puts a bottle of sleeping pills in his pocket, and in the loud jazz music, fixes his eyes on the enchanting body of the dancer Annie, greedily spitting words into her ear——

"Annie, you are so beautiful, your body is streamlined——"

"Ha, you said that tonight, but tomorrow night you probably won't even pay attention to people, right? You are this person—"

"Annie, you are so smart." (But, tomorrow, who knows tomorrow?) Reaching into his pocket, touching the bottle of sleeping pills, his heart seemed to fall into an ice cellar.)

The newspaper reported: "1935 streamlined new car arrives in Shanghai, reducing air resistance by 13%, speed: 75 miles per hour!"

——These days, even people's lives are streamlined ah.

Amateur Mailbox

Is It Okay to Marry a Prostitute? 263

Mr. Editor:

I am a young clerk in a shop, already twenty-two years old. I am not yet married. My family is in the countryside, and I am alone in Shanghai, so in my spare time, I am very free. Who knew that this freedom would cause my current problem!

Not long ago, due to the temptations of the environment and various stimuli, I ended up on the path of seeking pleasure. Soon, I met a prostitute. She has a gentle temperament and none of the licentious habits of prostitutes. I love her very much, and she sees my honesty. At the same time, knowing that she has fallen into this pit of fire and has little hope of getting out, for the sake of her lifelong happiness, she expressed her willingness to marry me. I understand everything about her and feel that she is a hardworking woman. So, driven by our emotions, we made a lifelong promise. Although we have privately agreed to marry, many problems have followed, making me feel doubtful and uncertain. I don't know what to do.

(1) This matter has not been approved by my parents. If they find out she is a prostitute, they will definitely encounter strong opposition. If relatives and friends know, they will certainly disapprove, which may affect my position.

(2) She has been a prostitute for more than two years. Will this affect her ability to have children in the future?

(3) According to my current financial situation, I cannot afford the cost of marriage. However, she is willing to endure another year of hardship to save some money, which can reduce my burden. But is this method feasible?

(4) If I break up with her, how can the wounds on my soul be healed?

Sir, because of these problems, I am hesitant. I wonder if you would give me a clear indication? Sincerely,

Respectfully submitted, Gao Xueqing

Editor's Note: In the minds of most people, prostitutes are considered the most lowly people because they can lead young men who venture into brothels to ruin, causing them to lose their fortunes and reputations. They seem to be an "inauspicious object." But this sin is not caused by prostitutes themselves. They are products of an abnormal society. They are pitiful creatures under economic oppression. We should sympathize with them. However, due to traditional concepts deeply rooted in people's hearts, people generally despise them.

Patronizing prostitutes is originally an act of self-degradation and is not worthy of emulation. But now, if one can repent and want to find someone to entrust their dissipated soul to, it may be the first step towards turning back. Therefore, although we do not rashly approve of marrying a prostitute, it is possible under special circumstances.

Mr. Gao said in his letter that his current financial situation cannot afford the cost of marriage. Then, where did the money for his past indulgence come from? Is it a misappropriation of public funds? (Although this cannot be confirmed, such behavior is inevitable when one is lost.) If so, he should immediately economize on his own expenses and try to make amends, so as not to be discovered later, which would leave him with nowhere to stand.

Now, let's discuss his four questions. The first question: a passive approach is to first redeem her. If she has family or relatives, she can temporarily stay with her relatives, and then go through formal marriage procedures. Besides, prostitutes and good women do not have obvious differences, and it will not be revealed for a while. Once the deed is done, the parents will not say anything. But from a positive perspective, as long as you have the ability to be independent in marriage and make a living, as long as she can consistently love you after marrying you, you don't have to care about other people's contempt and attacks. The second question: a doctor should be consulted immediately for an assessment. At the same time, her behavior should also be carefully observed to avoid harming future happiness. The third question is absolutely not feasible. Because a prostitute's life is like being in a pit of fire, how can you save someone from water and fire by delaying it? Moreover, "one who stays near vermilion gets stained red, and one who stays near ink gets stained black." In such a bad environment, her character is also often in danger of changing. As for economic difficulties, there is only the method of economizing, but since you see her as a hardworking woman, it may not be a problem.

As for the last question, it is fundamentally contradictory. We believe that if you have considered it and think it is worth marrying, then why talk about breaking up? If you think it is not worth marrying, then you have fundamentally lost the foundation of love, and even if you break up, there will be no pain.

Correction: There were many typographical errors in the handwritten manuscript published last Thursday. For example, "穀" was mistyped as "槖". "　" and "県" should be swapped. "鴻" should be changed to "鸿", "誠" to "诚", and so on.

Correction: Yesterday's illustration "迷亡" was a mistake for "逃"亡, we hereby correct it.

Ancient Prose 268

Wang Bingmei Donglai Bo Yi

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Yu Fu Assassinating Duke Yin (Continued)

The word "將" (will) is Duke Yin's greedy and cherish heart. It is a form of expression. It should be given immediately. Why is there a will to give? To plan a speculative opportunity? Hearing is immediate. How can there be a "will"? This is why it provoked Yu Fu's humiliation and aroused Duke Yin's suspicion, and ultimately led to his death. Alas, Duke Yin's righteousness of relinquishing the country, his heart is so clear, his deeds are so obvious. Even the slightest fault cannot be tolerated, and he suffered a great disaster. Moreover, those whose hearts and deeds are not as visible as Duke Yin's, how dare they not strive to do better? Therefore, the gentleman's pursuit of righteousness continues day and night, daring not to use his utmost efforts. It is not only to be familiar with righteousness but also to avoid disaster. Without the disaster of Duke Yin, pursuing it means that those who do righteousness are satisfied with establishing one virtue and cultivating one behavior. They are impatient and do not move forward. Therefore, it is said, "Encouraging the world to have a heart for righteousness is the assassination of Duke Yin."

Shenbao Local Supplement Movie Special

A Brief History of Film Development (13) 269

— Wen Ying

(13) Audience Reactions to Sound Films

When sound films were first invented, there was a wave of heated resistance among the audience. All they heard was a harsh, grating sound. Therefore, they felt that this new thing was too noisy, depriving them of the quiet enjoyment they had in the movie theater. In addition, there were many things they were unaccustomed to seeing and hearing. For example, their favorite big star, Conrad Nagel, suddenly started talking in a halting manner on the screen. And the sound of his voice seemed to come from his vest pocket. This made them feel involuntarily annoyed. We must know that when sound films were first invented, Conrad Nagel was one of the few actors who could speak correctly. Everyone was vying to hire them, but because of the imperfection of the machinery, their accents were messed up.

The earliest sound films were mostly short comedies, and some were newsreels. The actors in the short comedies were mostly vaudeville actors from the stage. But soon after, they added dialogue to the silent films. That kind of dialogue could make you jump out of your seat. Many actors you thought were very quiet and elegant suddenly shouted and clamored on the screen. And their voices were not meant to be melodious but went up and down, making people impatient.

Many conservative theater managers, after watching these early sound films, believed that this kind of thing was just a temporary fad and would not last long. They were unwilling to spend money to rent sound films, but they saw that the number of people in their own theaters was small, while the number of moviegoers in the theaters across the street was increasing day by day. Soon, they gradually followed others and adopted sound films.

As for Hollywood, it was originally a place most sensitive to light, so within a few months after the invention of sound films, there was a very violent disturbance. Hollywood's material concepts had completely changed. The noisy silent film studios had been dismantled. Great, quiet, sound-isolated sound stages were built.

We must know that silent film studios were never "silent." All the staff, from the director, lighting technicians, set designers, etc., were constantly talking loudly. But in the era of sound films, they could no longer "sound" off because the sound of a needle dropping on the ground would be as loud as a gunshot when recorded in the film.

At that time, there was a peak era of musical films. Hollywood's tycoons scoured for songwriting talents everywhere, but they soon realized that musical films were being overdone, and many songwriters lost their jobs and returned home. But among the actors, an outstanding talent rose at that time, which was also a romance in film history, an accidental occurrence. We probably still haven't forgotten the first sound and dance mega-production "The Jazz Singer." When Warner bought that script, preparing for their groundbreaking move, the actor in their mind was originally George Jessel. But when they discussed and signed the contract with George Jessel, negotiations broke down due to disagreements on the terms. The Warner Company then gave that contract to Al Jolson, a singer on Broadway in New York, a frustrated performer in decline.

After "The Jazz Singer" was released, Al Jolson jumped to become a hero created by the times. He was the most popular person of the era. He was the only hope for the future of sound films. He caused an unprecedented sensation, which was rare thereafter. He established special merits in a certain position. That is, he gave the makers of sound films a powerful stimulant and provided considerable consolation and encouragement to all those involved in the invention, advancement, and completion of sound films. (To be continued)

Review of "David Copperfield" 270

— Ji Han

David Copperfield

——Nanjing Screening

People are probably already shocked by the fame of Charles Dickens, and they know a lot about everything about him, so it seems unnecessary to introduce him again here. Taking a step back, from films such as "A Tale of Two Cities" or "Oliver Twist," audiences have long been deeply familiar with their style. Therefore, regarding "David Copperfield" on film, I only want to talk about some aspects of the technical presentation.

People usually say that it is not easy to express a novel of hundreds of thousands of words on more than ten thousand feet of film. In terms of capacity, it is obviously very difficult. Therefore, general literary films cannot but cut out some of the unimportant parts of the novel, otherwise, it can only be verbose and piled up.

On the other hand, novels can have exquisite psychological descriptions. This delicate psychological portrayal is something that drama and film cannot achieve, and it becomes a unique function of novels. Therefore, when adapting a novel into a film, one must try to express the inner descriptions outwardly, but this is very laborious work. — This illustrates that film has its unique skills. It breaks through the categories of time and space in drama. It must concretely convey all abstract words with images, so that the appreciators can obtain a more direct response.

In these areas, the author of "David Copperfield" can be said to have done it completely. This is excellent in all aspects of screenwriting, directing, acting, ... and is entirely expressed in terms of film art. In order to illustrate these points, I would like to cite a few examples as concrete proof.

(1) Little David playing at the fisherman's house. He and a little girlfriend are on the beach. The little girl said, "If I become a noblewoman, I will buy Uncle Bundy (the fisherman) a big blue coat, and that coat will be full of jewels." This dialogue shows that she harbors great extravagance. (This serves as a foreshadowing of her later infatuation with the young master.) Then she stands on a wooden board on the coast, whistling in the wind, seagulls soaring around her, and thin white clouds undulating and flying with the waves. This is a very good expression of her personality.

(2) After David returns home from Bundy, he begins to live a miserable life. Before he is beaten by his stepfather for not reciting his book, the director uses close-ups of the whip and his aunt's sewing needle to describe David's fearful state of mind. When we see him being beaten, we deeply sympathize with him and deeply hate that stepfather. Until his mother dies in her bed, it is a bleak dusk with bitter winds and rain. He escapes down like a prisoner, shouting loudly, which cannot but move people.

(3) David walks to his aunt's house, repeatedly using the meter to not explain the distance, and at the same time, explaining his hardships from his clothes. He immediately writes about his aunt's habit of driving horses to his aunt's house, which is as simple and lovely as Michael Burr's previous return home from the window to avoid debt. Later, when David tells his aunt about his various experiences, we shed tears of sympathy for him.

(4) Another thing to mention is that young David and his friends go to fisherman Bundy's house, just as Xiao Liu is secretly engaged. At this time, the singing of David's friend is not accompanied by music to show the simplicity of the countryside, which is also unique. Later, the storm and huge waves that engulfed the boat showed us excellent photographic technology.

The above are all more prominent and special places, which explains the success of "David Copperfield" in terms of expression methods. As for its nature, it is not within the scope of this article.

A Critique of "Babbitt" 271

— Zhao Ren

Babbitt——A Cathay Film Production

In reviewing "Babbitt," we must first address its original author, Sinclair Lewis. People will not forget that he was the recipient of the 1930 Nobel Prize in Literature, nor will they forget that he was the author of "Main Street."

Anyone who has read his works likely understands him to be a satirical writer. Whether in "Main Street" or "Babbitt," he used a satirical pen to depict the vulgar views of small-town philistines on the world, or to expose the ugliness of bourgeois and so-called upper-class gentlemen, or their mundane ways of conducting themselves.

Speaking of this, we cannot help but think of writers like Crendon or the veteran writer George Moore (the original author of "The Lake"), who also appeared in the guise of satirical writers. These two writers were able to expose the maladies of society from an economic perspective, using satirical pens to expose readers to profound and spicy ridicule, while on the other hand, they gave great sympathy to the oppressed and sacrificed in present society. Therefore, from a realistic point of view, they should receive extremely high honors; at least in America, they should be representatives of successful writers.

However, Lewis is the standard American bourgeois writer. He does not satirize or expose things from their essence; he only superficially satirizes the lack of morality of upper-class people. He believes that the wealthy gentlemen should not be treacherous and cunning. These things are delicate and refined depictions of the philistines he saw, while on the positive side, he actively supports the existing society, like a loyal servant mocking his master's tuxedo for not being elegant enough. Perhaps their master will dress neatly because of this mocking advice.

Now let's look at how he wrote in "Babbitt"? The protagonist, Babbitt, is a complete bourgeois with a vulgar outlook on life. He is infected with all the bad habits that philistines possess. And this kind of person is despised and played with in the upper class, but also exposes the filth of upper-class morality. Although these things have been somewhat deleted in the film's performance, we can still see him infatuated with women's letters, flattered to be embraced as a backbone of the Zebra Club, holding vulgar and unbearable views in the deliberations for establishing a library, associating with powerful figures to show off in front of his wife, and doing things he doesn't want to do in order to curry favor—scheming to buy land for future resale to the government at a high price. In reality, he is a vulgar coward who reveals his conspiracy at the sight of female beauty and is at a loss when threatened by women, almost wanting to commit suicide. He feels ashamed when he sees the newspaper's criticism of him, but fortunately, he has a capable wife who takes care of everything for him, covering up his ugliness and making him re-embraced by the people, so he is overjoyed again. Such a vulgar bourgeois is naturally a ridiculous figure in people's eyes. But what impression does this give people? Does it give people a clear and essential understanding of the Luo Hui of society? No, it just makes people laugh.

Due to the tight structure of the script in the film, due to the director's lack of attention to stiff shots, and due to the excellent acting skills of the lead actress, Aline MacMahon, this film is not without its merits. However, as a comedy, this film is not very lively, and there is too much dialogue, which inevitably makes people feel a little tired.

Film Novel

Amateur Reporter (After Office Hours) (2) 273

— Tong Yun

The girl laughed again and said, "Whatever you say." Jim glanced at her, feeling that this socialite was too arrogant. He was her superior, and he should show some of the colors of a superior. So he said solemnly, "How can it be whatever I say? You either are or you aren't, you can't just let others say you are. " The girl said, "You're right. I am Agnes... Nancy Sharon... but that's not my real name. Jim deliberately raised his eyebrows, looked at her, and said, "Royalty? Nobility? Hiding your name like this?"

Sharon knew he was teasing her, but she didn't seem to care and said, "Neither. My real name is Sharon Nugget." Jim said, "Nugget? Any relation to Mrs. Sailor Nugget of Newbold?" Sharon said, "That's my mother." Jim couldn't help but make a "wow" sound and asked her how long she had been working as a newspaper reporter. Sharon said, "Not long. But I know it's not a difficult thing." Jim lit a cigar himself, looking at her with his eyes half-open and half-closed. Her conceited attitude, her body full of fragrance, and her childish voice all made him feel uneasy, and he didn't like that kind of woman. Moreover, her blood-red lips and fashionable clothes aroused a sense of hostility in him.

He thought for a while and suddenly asked, "Do you like your work?" Sharon said. "Couldn't be better. There are unexpected interests. Of course, I can't limit myself to music reviews. I have to learn everything. I think the editing methods of a modern newspaper must be improved, and truly knowledgeable people must be used."

Jim listened to her and didn't say anything himself. He picked up a proof and pretended to look at it carefully. But Sharon continued to talk eloquently, "I think the News Record is a little more advanced than other newspapers, so I chose this newspaper as my place for practical experience. I think that no matter how sufficient a person's ideals are, experience is indispensable... Do you agree?" She said, smiling sweetly.

At this point, Jim was planning how to deal with this arrogant socialite. He coughed slightly, pretending to be attentive, and said, "Shall we order two cups of tea?" She knew he was making fun of her, but pretended not to know and said, "That couldn't be better." After she said that, she sat waiting for tea. Jim slowly looked at the proofs one by one, made two phone calls, but neither ordered tea nor paid attention to her. Sharon, on the other hand, continued to wait, not discouraged at all. She waited quietly for him, she wanted to discuss that music review. After waiting for a long time, she saw that Jim had nothing important to do except push the paper back and forth, so she took the initiative to say, "Didn't you see me to discuss that review?"

Jim was asked by her, and then raised his head and said, "Oh... that's right. That article is too... too wonderful... too profound. Of course, with your level, it's not difficult to write, mocking those old-fashioned people who like to listen to Beethoven's Fifth Symphony to the point of being completely defeated, but... my readers may not agree with your views." Sharon's face flushed, and she glared at him fiercely. It turned out that he had called her to make fun of her. She admitted that he was young and handsome, but the fact that he didn't take her seriously and used her the first time they met made her hate him from the bottom of her heart. (To be continued)
